planet Alsakan
	attributes agffa_20wonders agffa_city agffa_core agffa_galacticempire
	landscape land/unknown
	music ambient/hangar
	description "Alsakan was an ecumenopolis world in the Alsakan system in the Core Worlds. A Core Founder on the Perlemian Trade Route, Alsakan was an ancient, wealthy world that had been a major political player for centuries, and was responsible for the seventeen Alsakan Conflicts that had been fought with Coruscant over the nature and shape of the early Galactic Republic."
	spaceport `	The Alsakani were Human settlers who had arrived on the planet aboard the colony ship Kuat Explorer some twenty-six thousand years before the Battle of Yavin. As a people, they were aristocratic in their values and enthusiastic for open spaces and local independence. Consequently, they had sought a limited economic and political union when the Galactic Republic was formed, and for much of their history were inclined to see Coruscant as too powerful, resulting in the many Alsakan Conflicts. Reflecting their views, the ancient Alsakani national epic, the Archaiad, described the Perlemian Trade Route as "an arrow sent into the possible". Seeking distance from authority, Alsakan's younger sons established small colonies in the Inner Rim, and cared little for government bureaucracy or mass-produced goods beyond warships and blasters. The Alsakan Mosaics are tile mosaics found in the city of Rucapar on the planet Alsakan. The center of the mosaic is at the city square and extends as five lanes of tile to five equidistant mountains. Most of the original mosaic was destroyed during the Third Alsakan Conflict, only remnants have survived. However, it is included in the Twenty Wonders of the Galaxy by Vicendi in 10,000 BBY.`
	shipyard "Imperial Navy Ships"

Known as the "Defender of the Core", for millennia it was the site of the Republic Navy's primary fleet base and War College. It was considered the site of naval power, tradition and prestige by both the Galactic Republic and the Galactic Empire.`
	spaceport "	While not as industrialised as Axum, Anaxes was more prestigious, home to many families associated with a tradition of service in the Fleet. It was home to Azure Motorworks, a major producer of luxury vehicles. Considered an ecumenopolis, in that it was a planet-wide city, it was more reminiscent of a Green Coruscant, though, in that it was sprinkled with beautiful parks and green areas in and around the city like the Great Plain of Anaxes."

planet Arkania

	landscape land/unknown
	music ambient/hangar
	description "Arkania is the adopted homeworld of the Arkanians, a near human species. It is covered with tundra and is rich in diamonds and other precious minerals, which the Arkanians mined to further their offworld connections and master their technology. Arkanian cities are designed to keep the cold out and are almost completely enclosed. Off-world visitors rarely have to deal with the frigid conditions of the planet. Many citizens are miners."

planet Berchest
	attributes agffa_20wonders agffa_colonies agffa_galacticempire agffa_tourism agffa_trade
	landscape land/unknown
	music ambient/hangar
	description "Berchest is a major tourist destination and a trading planet, in the Anthos sector of the Inner Rim. It is an extremely beautiful world whose highly saline seas and strong tides resulted in immense crystal deposits on the planet's shores that the native Berchestians sculpted into entire cities. One of these cities is Calius saj Leeloo, or the City of Glowing Crystal. It was carved entirely from one massive crystal that was created over the centuries from salt deposits from the adjacent Leefari Sea and is considered one of the Twenty Wonders of the Galaxy."

planet Byss
	attributes agffa_deepcore agffa_galacticempire agffa_shipyard agffa_sith
	landscape land/unknown
	music ambient/hangar
	description "Byss was a planet in the Deep Core, near the center of the galaxy, discovered no earlier than 45 BBY. A local day lasted 31 standard hours, and a local year lasted 207 local days. It was the endpoint of the Byss Run. Byss itself was somewhat of a myth, seeming to be the perfect place to live. Its eerie blue-green glow, caused by its sun, also added to the strangeness of the world. Despite this outward appearance, however, Emperor Palpatine's dark-side energies were everywhere, corrupting not only the inhabitants, but the planet itself. Byss was the secret throne world of Palpatine and the location of his towering Imperial Citadel. He also kept his secret supply of clone bodies there."
	spaceport "	Byss was a mythic paradise world enshrouded in the dark side of the Force, located within the isolated and nearly inaccessible Deep Galactic Core. It was situated at the end of the Byss Run, a heavily guarded artificial hyperlane kept open by hundreds of non-mass S-thread boosters, connecting the planet to the Core Worlds. The planet was otherwise nearly impossible to reach safely through hyperspace, due to the high density of stars in the Deep Core and the constantly shifting patterns of the region's natural hyperlanes."
	shipyard "Imperial Navy Ships"

This protected the Gran society, but it also isolated the Gran on Hok and Malastare who had begun to form strong bonds to their new homes. The Gran colonies continue independently, continuing the strong social bonds of Gran society but with loosened social codes. Unfortunately, the looser social codes allow for more corruption in the upper levels of colonial Gran society.`

	spaceport "	Naboo is a small pastoral world in the Mid Rim, located near the border of the Outer Rim Territories. The native Gungans, who built their homes in the waters of Naboo, rarely venture into the core, fearing the ravenous sea beasts which reside in areas such as the Caves of Eleuabad. Despite this, certain Gungan navigators utilize time-honored trade routes through the planet's structure, which serve as the most expedient avenues to reach other areas of the planet. Naboo's interior is rich with plasma, a naturally-occurring energy unique to the planet, and this coupled with its lack of molten core gives Naboo a reputation as an enigma to astrophysicists, who regard the world's structure as an extremely rare phenomenon in the galaxy."

	spaceport "	When the Republic collapsed and the Galactic Empire seized control of the galaxy, Pantora was cut off from the rest of the galaxy. Struggling to come to grips with their new predicament, the Pantoran Assembly split into three factions: the Appeasers, the Republicans, and the Expansionists. The dominant faction, the traditionalist Republicans, believed the Empire stood in stark opposition to the core principles and values of the Pantoran culture."

Alien housing complexes and tenements feature ventilation shafts that sent wafts of ammonia into the streets. The Ring acts as a junction between the Corellian Trade Spine—which connects it to the planets Coruscant and Anoat—and the Biox Detour, which connects it to the planets Takodana and Malastare."

planet Tatooine
	landscape land/tatooine
	music ambient/hangar
	description "Tatooine was a sparsely inhabited circumbinary desert planet located in the galaxy's Outer Rim Territories. Part of a binary star system, the planet was oppressed by scorching suns, resulting in the world lacking the necessary surface water to sustain large populations. As a result, many residents of the planet instead drew water from the atmosphere via moisture farms. The planet also had no natural surface vegetation."
	spaceport "	Initially inhabited by native Jawa and Tusken Raider species, it saw a population explosion following the search for valuable mining deposits on the planet's silicate surface. The Hutt Clan also maintained a presence on Tatooine, with Jabba the Hutt owning a palace in the desert at least by the time of the Clone Wars."

planet "Telos IV"

	landscape land/telosiv
	music ambient/hangar
	description "Telos IV, often called simply Telos, is the fourth world within the Telos system, located in the Outer Rim's Kwymar sector. Situated on the strategically important Hydian Way hyperlane, Telos is both economically and politically important, connecting the Core Worlds to the Outer Rim. During the Clone Wars the planet was located deep within Separatist-controlled space. As such, the people of Telos have a deep set resentment of the Galactic Empire. Rebel sympathisers can always be found here."
	spaceport "	Thousands of years in the past, Telos' surface was devastated in an ancient conflict. Since then, a thousand year project known as the Telosian Restoration Project has been underway, transforming the barren surface with its highly corrosive atmosphere into a paradise, complete with Sacred Parks and National Parks which play a large role in tourism. This project called for the construction of an immense space known as Citadel Station, which houses much of the Telos' population."

	description "The Redoubt, formally the Chiss Redoubt, was a remote star cluster that was located in Chiss space, near the Utegetu Nebula, and that contained at least ten habitable planets and hundreds of stars. planet Ukio
	attributes "Rebel Alliance"
	landscape land/unknown
	music ambient/hangar
	description "Ukio is a well-known agriworld in the Ukio system of the Abrion sector and the homeworld of the Ukians. It serves as one of the top producers of foodstuffs for the Core Worlds. Ukio is located within a star system of the same name in the Abrion sector of the Outer Rim Territories region of the galaxy. It is situated on the Manda Merchant Route, a hyperlane that connected it to Rishi and Molavar. Ukio itself is a large, terrestrial planet with gentle winds, calm weather, and a mild climate, which features virtually no seasonal variation due to the world's slow rotation and low axial tilt. It has a breathable atmosphere and light gravity. Ukio's land consists of three major continents cut through by hundreds of rivers. An Ukian day lasts 22 standard hours and an Ukian year lasted 357 local days."
	spaceport "	Ukio is one of the best-known and most efficient agricultural planets in its sector, featuring a growing season which lasted most of its year and ideal conditions for the production of grain and other foodstuffs. Ukio's surface, originally dominated by rolling hills and wild grasses, has been almost entirely given over to food production, but still contains ample fallow land for future expansion of the industry. Hundreds of rivers provide natural irrigation, which has been expanded through the use of technology which harnesses and diverts them. Ukian farmland is carefully cultivated and painstakingly maintained for maximum output, and crop rotation is required by law to prevent the destruction of arable land. The world is governed by the Overliege, a hereditary monarch, and is defended by planetary shields, which were operated by the Ukian defence Service."

planet Zonama
	landscape land/zonama
	music ambient/hangar
	description "Zonama Sekot (Ferroan for 'World of Body and Mind') is a living, sentient world capable of traveling through space. Zonama was the planet itself, while Sekot was the living intelligence of Zonama. It is also the seed of the original Yuuzhan Vong homeworld, Yuuzhan'tar, which had been destroyed during the Cremlevian War."
	spaceport "	Zonama Sekot is a unique world. Its north polar region, a spot of pearl white is surrounded by an entire hemisphere of tropical jungles. The edge of the southern hemisphere is also covered by elegant wisps of wind which frequently brake free to form spinning storms."
